An Inspection of the Jinpu Railway Line After the War 69

From Xuzhou to Jinan by Xuzhou Journalists

A communication from Jinan regarding the battlefield conditions along the line. After the Central Army defeated the main force of the Jin Army on the Jinpu Railway Line, the results of battles at various points along the line are sufficient for our observation. Therefore, the Xuzhou press formed a post-war inspection group for the Jinpu Railway Line to inspect the north. At the same time, the Xuzhou headquarters also dispatched Kuang Jingyou and Zhang Jichun to inspect various situations along the Jinpu Railway Line. Consequently, they jointly boarded the train northward on August 29th. The sights and sounds observed are described below:

Passing Through the Defense of Qufu and Yanzhou. The journalists and others departed from Xuzhou by military train at 4:30 PM on the 29th. The train was heavily congested with military vehicles and moved slowly. On the morning of the 30th, the train passed Tengxian and they immediately saw the war trenches built by Ma Hongda's troops north of Tengxian. There were also earthen bags piled up at the Liangxiadian station. At 5:00 PM, they crossed Zou County and arrived at Yanzhou. The journalists and others stayed at the Zhongxing Company. According to various circles, Ziyang suffered heavily from the war, especially the northern and eastern areas. Ershilipu Village north of the city was the site of a fierce battle when the Jin Army attacked Yanzhou. The eastern area was where the Jin Army divided its forces to launch a side attack on Yanzhou when besieging Qufu. Investigations revealed that the war zone covered more than a hundred villages, with over forty people killed, over a hundred injured, and five or six hundred houses destroyed. Much of the grain was requisitioned by the Jin Army, and the number of civilian laborers and vehicles requisitioned was considerable. The wooden doors of the residents in the city were dismantled by the defending troops to provide materials for fortifications. On the morning of the 31st, they took rickshaws to Qufu, where traces of war were visible everywhere. On the way from Yanzhou to Qufu, they saw two war trenches, one built by Ma Baolin's troops to defend Yanzhou against the Jin Army, located more than ten miles east of Yanzhou, and the other built by the Jin Army to attack Qufu, located about half a mile west of Qufu. Beside the trenches, there were still many coffins abandoned by the Jin Army, marked with the words "Deceased officers and soldiers of a certain division and regiment of the Third Route Army." After entering the city, they first went to the Duke Yansheng's Mansion. Duke Yansheng, Kong Decheng, was only eleven years old. His relative, Kong Lianfang, accompanied him to respond. Kong was too young to speak fluently. Kong Lianfang said that the sacred sites of Qufu should never have been bombarded indiscriminately. When the Jin Army's Chuan Zuo-yi division besieged the city, they fired six or seven thousand shells into the city. How could a small city like Qufu withstand so many shells? Therefore, the Kong Temple, the Yan Temple, the city towers, and the people's houses were all severely damaged. Then they visited the Kong Temple, which was grand in scale. The Hall of Great Achievement, the Sleeping Hall, the walls, and the side halls all had shell marks. In the Sleeping Hall, a shell even hit the roof ridge, broke through the ceiling, and fell down, fortunately without exploding, otherwise the hall would have been reduced to rubble. After visiting the Yan Temple, many pine and cypress trees inside the gate were withered, and the destruction was particularly severe. Half of the Xiaoxiang Hall was destroyed by shells, and the statue of Yan was exposed to the sky. The Enjoyment Hall and the Sleeping Hall were all damaged, with bullet marks everywhere. After coming out, they inspected the city towers, all four gates of which had been destroyed by shells, and many houses had also been knocked down by shells. West of Kong Forest, there were also Jin Army trenches, directly connected to the war trenches outside the west gate, showing the Jin Army's determination to attack Qufu. In the evening, they took rickshaws back to Yanzhou. One morning, they accompanied Magistrate Shi of Ziyang to inspect the war situation in Yanzhou. They climbed the city tower and looked around. All around the city wall were war trenches, interspersed with machine gun positions. The city tower was equipped with cannon positions. The parapets of Yanzhou had been demolished the year before, and now they were rebuilt with bricks. Bags were requisitioned from the people in the city and filled with earth for cover. The wooden doors of the residents were also dismantled to cover the trenches. The houses of the residents near the city, which could have provided cover for the Jin Army attacking the city, were all demolished. Although the Jin Army only surrounded the north and east sides and did not reach the city walls, the losses to the people were already huge. According to Shi, these fortifications were initially built by Ma Baolin's troops. After Chief Commander Liu arrived in Yanzhou, he ordered further construction and sent staff to guide the work. The circumference of Yanzhou was twenty-eight li, with a covered trench every thirty paces, four cannon positions at the four gates, and a total of more than 70,000 bags requisitioned. All the wooden doors in the city were dismantled and used, so there was a saying in Yanzhou that the doors were not closed at night, which was actually because there were no doors to close. Only 600 yuan was allocated to compensate for the demolished houses near the city. Other requisitions and war zones were still awaiting compensation. It was estimated that 50 million catties of firewood were requisitioned, as well as more than 3,000 civilian laborers, more than 1,000 ox carts, and more than 2,000 hand carts. The firearms of the Ziyang police force were confiscated by Ma's brigade during the defense of the city and have not yet been returned. The local area has no possibility of self-defense. They have already sent a representative to meet with Chief Commander Ma to negotiate. If the firearms are not returned soon, the local area will have no way to cope. At noon that day, they left Yanzhou and headed north. (To be continued)

Execution of Liu Yun by the Wuhan Garrison Command 70

And the Publication of Liu's Confession. A communication from Hankou. The Wuhan Garrison Command recently captured Liu Yun, a member of the Communist Party and the Military Commission of the Five Provinces along the Yangtze River, in Hankou. After detailed interrogation, he was sentenced to death and executed by firing squad on the 7th. However, Liu's confession to the Garrison Command revealed the internal situation of Soviet Russia, the organization of the Communist Party in the Yangtze River region, and the tasks he was responsible for. Today (the 8th), the Garrison Command specifically published his confession so that the people of Wuhan could understand the crimes of the Communist Party. The following is a verbatim record: (Question) What is your name? How old are you? Where are you from? (Answer) My name is Liu Yun, pseudonym Suiwu. I am currently twenty-six years old and from Yizhang County, Hunan Province. Because I am engaged in secret work, I cannot use one name exclusively, so I also have three names: Liu Zhiming, Li Zhihao, and Song Tui. (Question) Who are the members of your family? What is their situation? (Answer) My family has always been small farmers. My mother passed away long ago, and my father is still alive, but I have not heard from him for several years, and the relationship has been severed. I heard that he is now bankrupt and in a bad state. (Question) What schools have you attended? (Answer) I have attended many schools, and my thinking has changed accordingly. It should be divided into two points: (1) The schools I attended. Before the age of seventeen, I studied at a higher primary school in my county. At the age of seventeen, I joined the Franco-Chinese Work-Study Society and worked in a factory in Paris. Later, I entered aviation school. In the twelfth year, I returned to Guangzhou, transferred from the Jiangxi Army Lecture Hall to the first class of the Whampoa Military Academy, briefly served as a trainee in the teaching regiment, and was assigned to work in the Aviation Bureau. Later, I served as the director of education and the party representative of the air squadron in the aviation school. I participated in the Eastern Expedition. In September of the fourteenth year, I was sent to Soviet Russia by the National Government to study aircraft and military affairs. I transferred to the Army University after a year in the military aviation school, focusing on military research for more than three years. I graduated and returned to China in May of this year. (2) The changes in my thinking. When I was in high primary school in my county, I was inspired by the patriotic enthusiasm of the May Fourth Movement. I believed that the crisis of saving China could only be solved by strengthening the military, so I decided to go abroad to study military affairs. Unexpectedly, after arriving in Paris, because I had no government introduction, I could not enter any military schools. This was a blow to me. At the same time, I saw that the sophistication of European and American weapons was something that the Chinese had never dreamed of, and that aircraft were particularly necessary for combat, so I joined an aircraft factory to study the structure and principles of aircraft in practice. In 1922 (i.e., the eleventh year), I saw through the changes in material civilization and the treacherous competition among the imperialists. I realized that the narrow idea of enriching the country and strengthening the military was ultimately not feasible, so I joined the Socialist Youth League in Paris. In 1923, I returned to China and joined the Chinese Communist Party. At the same time, I also joined the Kuomintang. After arriving in the Soviet Union, my spirit was absolutely entrusted to the Third International. (Question) Did you receive any mission from the Third International when you returned to China this time? Who did you contact? (Answer) My return to China this time was a mission from the Third International to have me return to specialize in military work and reorganize the Red Army in China. When I set off in Moscow, Qu Qiubai told me to stay in Harbin and wait. Someone would naturally come to contact me. After staying in Harbin for three or four days, someone came and told me to stay at the Xinmin Hotel in Shanghai and someone would come to find you. After I arrived, I stayed for two weeks. Someone surnamed Wang came to contact me and moved to another hotel for a week. I was sent to Wuhan by the Central Committee of the Chinese Communist Party, so my arrival at that place and my contact with that person were all designated in advance by the Central Committee of the Communist Party. That is, when we met, we only asked each other's names. The truth or falsehood of the names and the place of residence were not investigated. If we wanted to investigate, not only would there be no result, but it would also cause suspicion among comrades. These are all the secrets of our party that should be absolutely observed. (Question) What is your position? (Answer) I am a member of the Military Commission of the Five Provinces in the Yangtze River region, and concurrently the chief of general staff. Four or five days ago, the Central Committee also entrusted me with the responsibility of organizing the 25th Red Army. (Question) How many people are in charge of the Military Commission? Where is the organization located? (Answer) There are three responsible members of the Military Commission. In addition to me, there is one called Zhang Jun and one called Wang Yuan, but our names are always changing, and we never use real names. They tell me false names, and I only tell you what they say. Please do not investigate further. However, if you insist on me saying it, I will just say it for what it is worth. As for our organization, it has not really been established yet. I wanted to build it earlier, but because renting a house in Hankou required a wife, I lost my deposit three or four times and was unable to rent a house. If I had rented a house, it would not have been so easy to catch me this time. As for the military plan for the five provinces, because I have not been in Hankou for long and the situation in various places has not been investigated clearly, it has not yet been drafted. (Question) According to people in your party, the Yangtze River Military Commission has been established for a long time. How could there be no organization? (Answer) The Military Commission has been in operation for more than two months, but the person in charge before was Cai Zhongxi, the commander of the 7th Red Army. His attitude was very passive and he did not actively organize, so the Central Committee was deeply dissatisfied and called me to take over. I have only been here for two weeks. Since I cannot rent a house, I cannot establish an organization. (Question) Where are the basic troops of your 15th Army? (Answer) I was arrested only three or four days after receiving the mission to organize, and I have not yet started planning. However, the basic troops referred to by the Central Committee are the peasants in various counties in southern Hubei. (Question) What have you been doing since you came to Wuhan? You must be familiar with the activities of the Communist Party here and the various organizations in the Yangtze River region. Tell us about it. (Answer) I am specifically responsible for military affairs and have no connection with the party affairs of various provinces, so I do not know the members and their activities at all. As for the organization in the Yangtze River region, it is divided into two types: one is the Political Committee, which is divided into guidance and adjudication departments, and the other is the Military Commission, which is divided into staff, worker-peasant armed forces, and reporting departments, all of which are concurrently held by the members. As for what I have been doing since I came to Hankou, there is nothing much because I have not completed the investigation and do not understand the situation. However, in the military aspect, I have actually been to Snake Mountain and stayed in the alarm clock tower for two nights. I have also been to Tortoise Mountain. I know the situation in these two places. (Question) Who is in charge of the Political Committee? (Answer) I have only met with someone surnamed Zhang twice, and I do not know the others. (Question) What is the recent organizational system of the Communist Party? (Answer) It is roughly divided into three departments: party affairs, politics, and military affairs, which are roughly the same at all levels. (Question) Who are the people in charge of the Central Committee of the Communist Party? (Answer) There are five members: Xiang Zhongfa, Li Lisan, Liu Changqun, and two peasants. Xiang Zhongfa also serves as the secretary. (Question) Recently, I heard that the Central Committee of the Communist Party has plans to move to Wuhan, Yuezhou, or Honghu. Is this true? (Answer) We have not received any notification or news of this. I do not know yet. However, based on my personal speculation, many people who know Li Lisan and Xiang Zhongfa are recognized here. Under these circumstances, they will definitely not move here casually. As for other places, there are more inconveniences for commanding work, and there is no possibility of establishing a foothold. (Question) You have been in Soviet Russia for a long time. What is the situation in that country? (Answer) Inside Soviet Russia, the cadre faction and the Trotsky faction have been in fierce conflict over the past year. As a result, Trotsky failed and was expelled. The brewing has continued to this day, and the disaster is still lurking, causing all facilities to be suspended. In terms of economics, there is often a bread panic. However, the cadre faction still advocates external development and encourages the Communist Parties of various countries to actively agitate, sparing no effort. Therefore, the money to support foreign Communist Parties is also spared no effort. However, in the military aspect, the progress is extremely rapid, and aviation tactics are particularly special. (Question) Have the people of Soviet Russia actually broken the concept of the state in practice? (Answer) Although the political appearance of Soviet Russia is called the World Cannon, the concept of the state still remains in the minds of the general public. That is, the actions of overseas Chinese from various countries are ultimately not as free as those of their own nationals. However, the cadre faction is working hard to correct this. (Question) Do you sympathize with murder and arson? (Answer) Murder and arson are certainly the immaturity of party members, but usually the local tyrants and bullies oppress the peasants and workers too much. Once this is reversed, it will evolve into revenge involving murder and arson, which is an inevitable part of the process. (Question) Looking at your situation, you certainly cannot be called talented, but you are not a waste either. However, you have been away from the country for too long, and you are not familiar with the situation in the country at all. You have also been too anesthetized by the Moscow Communist Party, so Director He and our Chief of Staff Ye are very sympathetic to you. If you can not violate the teachings of our Premier, the Director and the Chief of Staff may be able to help you. Think about it carefully. (Answer) I am not a talented person, and there is no need to be sympathetic. I am a firm believer in my doctrine. Please do not say any more. I only ask to be killed as soon as possible. However, the Communist Party has lost one person like me, although it will suffer some losses, but if I had been caught two or three weeks later, and my plans had been drafted successfully, then the credit of the Investigation Department, I believe, would have been much greater than it is now.

A Bizarre Drama During Li Jihong's Inauguration Ceremony 71

Xie Wugang Insults Zhang Guanshi. A communication from Hankou. Li Jihong, the special commissioner of finance in Hubei, held his oath-taking ceremony at the special commissioner's office on the 8th of this month. Many dignitaries from various circles attended, making it a grand occasion for a time. Unexpectedly, during this solemn ceremony, Zhang Guanshi, the director of the Hubei Finance Department, was suddenly slapped in the face by Xie Wugang, a guest, with the sound reverberating throughout the room. A bizarre drama thus occurred. The following is a record of the event:

The Bizarreness of the Speech. At 10:00 AM on the 8th, Li Jihong held a supplementary oath-taking ceremony. First, Xi Debing, the supervisory commissioner of the Ministry of Finance, delivered an instruction speech. Then, Chen Huren, the representative of the Provincial Government, and Li Shaoyang, the representative of the Acting Headquarters, successively delivered speeches, mainly stating that Special Commissioner Li was rich in financial management experience and would surely achieve good results in organizing the national taxes of Hubei in the future. They hoped that he would carry forward the revolutionary spirit and move forward. Then, Xie Wugang also stood up and gave a speech, roughly saying that comrades of the Party engaged in political work should act in accordance with the oath. Financial personnel should be especially clean and self-disciplined, and abide by the law. Zhang Nanxian and Li Jihong, the former directors of the Hubei Finance Department, could not be said to have been law-abiding. Now that Comrade Li is once again appointed as the special commissioner of finance, it is hoped that he will vigorously change his past mistakes and not be corrupt. After the speech, the onlookers were greatly surprised and suspected that Xie had a mental illness.

The Circumstances of the Instigation. After the oath-taking ceremony, Li invited the guests to the garden for a photo to commemorate the occasion. As Zhang Guanshi stood up to leave, Xie immediately followed closely behind him, loudly asking how much opium he had smoked this morning. Zhang replied that he had eaten a catty, using this to scold him. Xie also said that he had sent a gift to the director, but why had he not received a reply? Zhang replied that he had not received it. Xie said that he had sent it to the director's wife. Zhang said that he was being too shameless in his provocation. Before he could finish speaking, Xie's right palm had already landed on Zhang's left cheek. After the incident, Xie left with his head held high, while Zhang maintained his calm attitude and took pictures with the guests. Only after taking the pictures did he return to his private residence in anger.

Post-Incident Telegrams and Letters. After returning to his private residence, Zhang telegraphed He Chengjun in Luohe to report the incident, roughly saying that at 10:00 AM today, Hubei Special Commissioner Li held his inaugural ceremony, and he was invited to attend. Suddenly, someone who had represented the guests and delivered a speech ambushed him in public during the photography session and almost injured him. He asked that the person be arrested on the spot, but he was allowed to wander away. Although he himself was irrelevant, as a representative of both the military and political sides, he had no legal protection. Therefore, the government's prestige and local discipline would be completely swept away. Looking to the future, he could not help but feel cold and hoped that the reactionaries would be severely punished to rectify discipline. At the same time, the Special Commissioner of Finance's office also sent a letter to the Municipal Government and the Wuchang Public Security Bureau, requesting that Xie Wugang be arrested and brought to justice. The letter said that our Special Commissioner held a supplementary oath-taking ceremony on the second floor of the Bank of China in Hankou at 10:00 AM today. After the ceremony, he invited the guests to the photography session to take pictures as a souvenir. Suddenly, a thug named Xie Wugang insulted Director Zhang in the photography session, disrupted the order, and fled in a hurry, failing to be captured on the spot. The Director of your Municipality is requested to quickly order a search for his arrest and handle the matter in accordance with the law and report back.

Condolences from Dignitaries. Li Jihong and Liu Wendao took a car to Zhang Xuguan's private residence at No. 35 New Paris Street that evening to offer their condolences repeatedly. At the same time, many people came to offer their condolences, and the threshold was worn through. Today (the 9th), Zhang did not attend the 56th Provincial Government meeting and submitted his resignation. Although the Provincial Committee meeting decided to retain him, Zhang's anger seemed to not have subsided.

Xie Wugang Strikes Back. Xie Wugang had served in the military and had a violent temperament, but he was also quite straightforward. After this incident occurred, not only did he not try to escape, but he also went to court to accuse Zhang of dereliction of duty. Furthermore, on the 9th, he issued a declaration, stating his residential address in detail and hiring people to distribute it in Wuhan. The people of Wuhan, hearing of this strange event, all wanted to see what was going on and rushed to read it. The distributors temporarily set the price at four copper coins per copy, but the buyers were still very enthusiastic, and they quickly sold out. All the workers hired made three times their profit, which was also an interesting anecdote in this storm. (September 9th)

The Breach of the Yellow River Civil Embankment in Shandong 72

A communication from Jinan. The Liaoqiao civil embankment on the upper reaches of the Yellow River was breached due to continuous rising water. The civil embankment was supposed to be repaired under the supervision of the government and by the people, but the area happened to be at the intersection of Fan County, Shouzhang County, and Yanggu County, so the people of the three counties shirked responsibility to each other and refused to repair it, causing the breach to widen and the situation to become dangerous. The following is a record of the telegram from the dike defense committee: To the Director of the River Affairs Bureau, The mouth of the Liao embankment has widened to more than 130 zhang in recent days, with a water depth of 1.5 to 1.6 zhang, and the flow is three points, gradually expanding. The dike defense officer and section chief Zi Qian have repeatedly urged the county magistrates of Fan, Shou, and Yang to convene gentry and directors to discuss solutions. On the 17th of this month, the gentry and directors of Shou and Yang met in Fan County. The dike defense officers and others tried their best to mediate, almost to the point of exhaustion, but the gentry and directors of the three counties still looked at each other and there was no result or solution. At this time, the autumn flood is growing, and the river water is surging. The breach location is also at the top of a bend. If the main current moves into the adjacent river, not only will the villages along the river become a swamp, but the entire embankment of more than 100 li will also be filled with dangerous works. It is fortunate that the current has not yet completely shifted, and we should immediately start by lining the upper and lower parts of the mouth to prevent further expansion, so as to wait for the breach to be closed after the autumn. This should be more effective with less effort. However, the gentry and directors of each county do not care about the overall situation and are looking ahead without action. The dike defense officers and others are unable to reach them, and the situation has become helpless. We can only earnestly request that you quickly telegraph the county magistrates of Fan, Shou, and Yang to strictly urge the gentry and directors of each county to hold another emergency meeting to facilitate action and protect the people. [signed] Dike Defense Officer Zheng Jitai, Section Chief Zhou Ziqian, bowing, (September 5th)

An Overview of the Fisheries Administration in Jiangsu Province 73

The administrative measures for the fisheries industry in Jiangsu Province have been specified in the policy guidelines for the nineteenth year of the agricultural temple, such as the establishment of provincial fisheries experimental farms, marine research institutes, and preliminary fisheries facilities in Haizhou, Xinyang Port, Lusi Port, Hupu, Shengshan (representing Shanghai), etc. Although it is not easy to proceed due to the province's financial difficulties, the department is still actively planning and has not slackened. The following is a brief description of the progress:

Investigation of Coastal Fisheries and Patrol Vessels. The Department of Agriculture believed that the existing fisheries in the coastal counties of the province had not yet been fully investigated. In addition to the establishment of the Shengshan Fisheries Experimental Farm and the Marine Research Institute, which are important facilities, the nineteenth-year policy guidelines for the fisheries sector call for the establishment of fisheries guidance centers in the prosperous fisheries areas of the coastal counties. Therefore, a preliminary investigation is an important task. On the 8th of last month, Promotion Officer Zhang Yousheng was dispatched to Chongming, Haimen, Qidong, Nantong, and other four counties to investigate the existing fisheries as a reference for the future establishment of guidance centers. The Department also believed that the relationship between coastal defense and fisheries was close, so it sent a letter to the Wusong Coastal Patrol Office to investigate the tonnage, speed, draft, number of crew members, armed equipment, and 24-hour fuel consumption, and total monthly expenditure of the patrol vessels under its jurisdiction and those frequently traveling to Jiangsu, and to report back in detail as a reference for coastal defense in the province.

Preparation for the Provincial Fisheries Experimental Farm. The Department of Agriculture believed that the establishment of the Provincial Fisheries Experimental Farm in the province had long been included in the eighteenth-year budget, and a preparatory office had been set up, with a commissioner appointed to be responsible for the handling, but it could not proceed due to the province's financial difficulties. Recently, in light of the fact that Japanese fishing boats frequently come to our Jiangsu territorial waters to fish illegally, it is necessary to establish the farm as soon as possible. It was again submitted to the 315th meeting of the Provincial Government, and it was resolved and approved to start preparations immediately. Last month, Wang Wentai, the former director of the Haizhou Aquatic Products Experimental Farm of the Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce, was added as a preparatory officer and went to Shanghai to actively prepare and speed up the process in order to establish it as soon as possible.

Formulation of Model Articles of Association for Fisheries Associations. The Department of Agriculture believed that the Fisheries Association Law had been promulgated by the National Government and came into effect on July 1. As a result, fishermen in various counties have been organizing fisheries associations and applying for registration. However, the articles of association they drafted were mostly unusable. To save guidance procedures, the Department specifically formulated model articles of association for fisheries associations in various counties in Jiangsu Province, and guidelines for the preparation of fisheries associations in various counties in Jiangsu Province, and printed and distributed them to various counties so that fishermen could follow them and organize associations according to law.

Collection of Models of Offshore Fishing Boats. The forms and structures of fishing boats in this province are extremely complex. The Department of Agriculture specifically instructed the county governments of Chuansha, Songjiang, Nantong, Nanhui, Dongtai, Rugao, Yancheng, Funing, and other eight counties to take the various important fishing boat styles, materials, and dimensions of each part of the various sea-based boats under their jurisdiction and make scaled-down models according to a ratio of one-tenth for small fishing boats and one-twentieth or one-thirtieth for large fishing boats, and attach a full set of scaled-down models of the fishing gear used, along with explanatory notes, for research purposes.

Local Communications Songjiang 74

The Urgent Expansion of the Police Brigade. Our county is located in the center of the Shanghai-Hangzhou transportation hub, with access to all directions. Cases of robbery and kidnapping are reported from various villages from time to time. Local security consists only of one police company, which is often insufficient to mobilize when the villages are alarmed by bandits. The second county administrative meeting resolved to expand the county police into a large brigade, and the operating expenses are planned to be raised from wealthy households in the form of protection donations, which have been submitted to the provincial department for approval. After receiving the document, County Magistrate Jin ordered the district chiefs to select recruiters, who were hired by the county on file. It is now known that because the matter has been going on for a month, the actual number of recruits in each district has not yet been reported. A fast telegram was sent to the district chiefs to proceed quickly and to submit a report on the recruitment process before the 20th of this month.

Relocation of the 15th Substation to Caojing. Punan Shanyang and Caozhe in this county are all coastal areas where bandits come and go unpredictably. The local people applied for and were approved to establish the 15th Public Security Substation, which was organized and established in Shanyang last month and started operating. However, it is heard that the central area should be Caojing, and the housing police donations, which are used as a source of funds, are also more numerous in Caojing. Previously, the people of Caojing applied to the county government, which forwarded the request to the Public Security Bureau, and it was approved to relocate the 15th Substation to Caojing and set up a police station in Shanyang under the jurisdiction of the substation. The order has been forwarded for implementation.

Suzhou 75

Regarding Suspicion of Reactionary Activities, Requesting Instructions from the Provincial Authorities for Disposition: After the Public Security Bureau's bicycle patrol officers Wang Du and Yu captured a suspected counter-revolutionary, Song Qin, on the anniversary of July 7th, they arrested Song Zhao-cai, Kong Shao-xi, and fifteen others. Yesterday (the 10th), the Judicial Section of the Public Security Bureau interrogated them. Song Qin confessed that he was in charge of propaganda for the Suzhou County Sports Committee, and Kong Shao-xi was the secretary. He also confessed that he had attended several meetings at the Fang Sheng Temple in the southern suburbs of the city. The abbot of the temple, Monk Songlin, also participated in the meetings. Songlin has also been taken into custody. After Zhang, the section chief, recorded the confessions, he instructed his subordinates to continue to secretly apprehend those involved and submitted a report to the provincial government for instructions.

The Water Police Capture Bandits Who Looted Wuzhen: Huai Zongbang, the captain of the 14th team of the Water Police, recently received a tip that Wang Chuanzhi, a bandit involved in the Wuzhen looting case, and a monk were hiding outside the East Gate of Wujiang. Captain Huai, acting on the tip, immediately ordered a secret investigation and apprehended Wang, handing him over to the Wujiang County Government for investigation. Yesterday, he submitted a report to the Third District for instructions.

Sentencing of a Large Number of Reactionary Criminals: The Second Criminal Court of the Higher Court yesterday sentenced a large number of counter-revolutionary criminals. Chen Xiaosan was sentenced to four years of imprisonment for the crime of assisting in the propagation of doctrines incompatible with the Three Principles of the People. Gao Shoufeng was sentenced to eleven months of imprisonment for the crime of joining a counter-revolutionary gathering. Zhao Fengming was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the same crime. Chu Guan-ke was sentenced to eleven months of imprisonment for the crime of joining a counter-revolutionary organization. Ding Sijing and Yan Dunshi were each sentenced to five months of imprisonment. Lin Lou was sentenced to six months of imprisonment.

Merchants and Residents of Guanqian Petition: Residents south of Guanqian Street, concerning the Zhao Wall of the Xuanmiao Temple, which the provincial government has ordered the Construction Department to demolish according to the original plan, dispatched nine representatives, including Xu Xunru, to the County Government yesterday afternoon at 1 p.m. They petitioned the County Government to instruct the Construction Bureau to inform Abbot Yan to immediately demolish the wall in order to expedite the reconstruction of city buildings and see the temple's early completion. County Magistrate Huang responded that the case was still under consideration, and execution would begin as soon as the final decision from the provincial government was received. The representatives left satisfied.

Proposed Names for the Ring Road: The Public Security and Construction Bureaus have jointly proposed the following new names for the ring road: (1) From Qian Wanli Bridge to Xinmin Bridge, it will be called Xinmin Road. (2) From Xinmin Bridge to Guangji Bridge, it will be called Guangji Road. (3) From Guangji Bridge to Wanyuan Bridge, it will be called Puyi Road. (4) From Wanyuan Bridge to Shilukou, it will be called Fuan Road. (5) From Wanyuan Bridge to Yongfu Bridge, it will be called Yongfu Road. (6) From Yongfu Bridge to Nanxin Bridge, it will be called Minxing Road. (7) From Shilukou to Aihe Bridge, it will be called Beijinchan Road. (8) From Aihe Bridge to Xiaorihui Bridge, it will be called Nanjinchan Road. (9) From Xiaorihui Bridge to Tairang Bridge, it will be called Tairang Road. (10) From Tairang Bridge to Gordon Bridge, it will be called Xujiang Road. (11) From Gordon Bridge to Wumen Bridge, it will be called Sutai Road. (12) From Wumen Bridge to Gantang Bridge, it will be called Qingyang Road (or Panxi Middle Road for both sections). (13) From Gantang Bridge to Midu Bridge, it will be called Chilan Road. (14) From Midu Bridge to Xugong Bridge, it will be called Xiexi Road. (15) From Xugong Bridge to Jiangmentang, it will be called Jiangmentang. (16) From Jiangmentang to Baji Bridge, it will be called Loujiang Road. (17) From Baji Bridge to Qimen Drawbridge, it will be called Donghui Road. (18) From Qimen Drawbridge to Qian Wanli Bridge, it will be called Xihui Road.

Fengxian 76

Reporting the Establishment of the Four-County Joint Defense: The Five-County Joint Defense plan initiated by this county was ordered to convene a meeting in Fengxian on the 6th of this month. At that time, because Jinshan was not present, it was discussed and changed to a four-county joint defense of Songjiang, Fengxian, Shanghai, and Nanhui. It was also decided to establish a joint defense office immediately, with County Magistrate Shen Qingchen as the director. In addition to the two members jointly recommended by the party and government organs of this county, the members recommended by each county were Zhang Qianshou for Songjiang, Ding Jien for Shanghai, and Cai Zhuocheng for Nanhui. The Water Public Security Team sent Liu Zhao, the captain of the first battalion of the first district, to join. In addition, the party departments of each county were also invited to participate in the meeting. The monthly expenditure was temporarily set at 120 yuan, which was apportioned by each county for use. County Magistrate Shen has personally taken the approved regulations to the province today to present everything in person.

Soliciting Customs Surplus Treasury Bonds: The quota for this county's customs surplus treasury bonds was originally set at 60,000 yuan, but after Director Wang Zhuofu of the Finance Bureau personally went to the province to present the desolate situation, it was approved to be reduced to 40,000 yuan. According to the previous practice of allocating 20 yuan for every 100 mu of land, the bureau dispatched personnel yesterday to cooperate with the district offices to collect the bonds and issued temporary receipts from the county bureau, which will be adjusted later.

Jiashan 77

Eleven Floating Corpses Discovered in Xia Mutang: The military and police jointly suppressed bandits, and the Zhi Guo warship provided cover with artillery fire. The number of bandits killed at that time is impossible to determine. Yesterday, eight floating corpses were discovered in the Xia Mutang area. The corpses were all wounded by bullets. Three of the corpses still had Mauser pistols, etc. attached. The local farmers reported the discovery and went to examine the corpses for investigation.

Lake Bandits Loot Two Major Towns: Detailed Report on the Robbery in Tianren Town and Youchegang: Tianren Town in Jiashan County and Youchegang in Jiaxing County were looted by lake bandits at 4:30 a.m. on the 7th. This has already been reported. According to detailed investigation, the lake bandits first destroyed the telephone lines when they arrived in the town, and then went to the Public Security Bureau and the Self-Defense Corps to confiscate firearms. They used a ladder to climb from the roof of the Ruiyu Salted Fish Shop into the Tongde Pawnshop and looted more than 1,000 yuan in silver dollars, ornaments worth about 400 yuan, and more than 100 pieces of clothing. Hengchang Qianzhuang was looted for more than 8,000 yuan in silver dollars, and two shop assistants and Xu Shaopeng, who went to Jiashan Hengtaifeng Cloth Shop to collect debts, were kidnapped. Also, the mistress of Xu Yongli Foreign Goods Shop was kidnapped for scolding the bandits, and the owner of Yufeng Clothing Shop, Zhou Ziming, and his partner, Gu Zhongyu, were kidnapped. Furthermore, Hu Zhuming was kidnapped to Qinglong Bridge near Taozhuang. He happened to encounter the suppression troops, and the two sides exchanged fire. He took the opportunity to escape. This time, more than 50 shops were looted, excluding teahouses and hotels, and dozens of households were looted, with a total loss of more than 50,000 yuan. In Youchegang Town, three rice shops, several South goods sauce gardens, and clothing shops were looted. Because it was late, the bandits were afraid of being surrounded and arrested by the police, so they dared not loot further and retreated. The Jiaxing Bandit Suppression Headquarters, the Water Police District Department, the Security Team stationed in Jiashan, and the County Public Security Bureau all dispatched teams to pursue and suppress them upon hearing the alarm. Four bandit boats and two bandit corpses were seized, along with one quick-firing gun and two wooden-cased guns. The remaining bandits scattered and fled. All the shops in Tianren Town were closed due to the huge losses this time. On the morning of the 9th, the Director of the County Public Security Bureau went to the town to persuade the shops to open together with the head of the District Public Office. The shops opened on the same day. He also went to the Tongde Pawnshop to investigate and dispatched the Director of the Ye Public Security Branch to the district head to supervise the loss from the 10th. At the same time, the local government wired the province to request troops to be stationed in the town to deter bandits.

Correction to the Communication on the 8th: In the looting case of the two towns, it was reported that the kiln owner Zhou Xuezhi was kidnapped. According to detailed investigation, this was indeed a misrepresentation. However, those who were omitted from the kidnapped included Xiao Dong, who was collecting debts for Jiashan Hengtaifeng.

Wuxi 78

Grocery Store Employee Runs Away Due to World-Weariness: Hong Da, the 19-year-old son of Gao Shengrong, a resident of Banqiao Township, Eighth District (Huaixia City), is currently working as an employee in the Rongchang Grocery Store in Rongxiang, Kaiyuan Township. He is usually diligent in his store duties, so he is highly valued by the store owner, Chen Bingkang. Recently, Hong Da suddenly changed his usual behavior and often lamented the suffering of his life. He also repeatedly told people about going out to join the army. The matter was heard by the store owner, who often advised and comforted him. Unexpectedly, his father, Shengrong, suddenly fell ill at home the other day, and the illness was dangerous. After Hong Da heard about it, he became even more saddened and suddenly developed a sense of world-weariness. He immediately wrote a suicide note on the counter, behind people's backs, and asked Chen Bingkang, the store owner, for leave yesterday morning. The store owner approved it, and Hong Da set off for home at noon. When he arrived near the Guandi Temple on Kaiyuan Road, he entrusted someone to take the suicide note to the Rongchang Grocery Store. The original letter roughly stated that his father's illness was incurable, and his family was heavily in debt. He originally intended to commit suicide in Wuxi, but was afraid that his family would come to collect the body after hearing about it, which would cost a lot of money, so he decided to go to Shanghai to commit suicide. After reading the letter, the store owner, Chen Bingkang, immediately sent people to search for him everywhere. He also made a long-distance call to Gao Liangsheng, his younger brother, at the Dechang Iron Store of the Tianhou Palace Bridge in Shanghai, ordering him to look for Hong Da's whereabouts in Shanghai.

Accusation of Fraudulently Obtaining Money by Setting Up a Silk Factory: Chen, the accountant of a silk cocoon storage in Liangxi Road outside Guangfu Gate in Xiyi, is skilled in calculation and has become well-off. Recently, he set up a Rui Da Silk Factory Preparatory Office in Beitang outside the North Gate. A certain Jia from Fenshui Dun, Yixing County, recently unemployed at home and eager to find a job, asked Zhu to transfer 1,000 taels of shares in Rui Da Silk Factory to Chen, who was doing business in Shanghai. Chen agreed and gave a temporary receipt. Unexpectedly, Chen was preparing to raise a capital of 30,000 taels, but he could not raise the full amount, so he changed the name to Xuchang Run Silk Factory, and Jia waited for a long time after exchanging a share certificate. He did not see it implemented, so he negotiated with Chen. Chen avoided seeing him, and Jia has now hired Lawyer Hu Jiayu to sue the County Government, accusing Chen of setting up a situation to collapse. After hearing the news, Chen, who was in Shanghai, rushed back to Xiyi from Hankou and surrendered himself. The County Government opened a court yesterday to detain Chen, who wanted to open a silk factory, to investigate.

The Overwhelming Cost of the Xin Cheng Road Repair Project: The southern section of the Xin Cheng Road, which began construction on April 3rd of last year, was not open to traffic until the ceremony held on August 20th of this year. Public long-distance buses travel. However, the roadbed from Tangtou to Yanqiao is not high and the soil is loose, making it dangerous for heavy vehicles to travel. Therefore, it was once suspended. Director Yao Dixi, of the Construction Bureau, recognized this difficulty and wanted to repair it, but the cost was enormous. The income from the toll fees, etc., must be remitted to the province, and cannot be retained in Wuxi for subsidies. However, the purchase of a large soil compactor requires about 10,000 yuan, plus the cost of coal dust and labor, for a total of more than 10,000 yuan. The bureau has no money. In order to complete the entire road, he took a car to the province on the morning of the 10th to ask Director Sun of the Construction Department for instructions on how to do it.

Jiangyin 79

Li Hongze's Case Will Be Transferred to Suzhou: Li Hongze, the former inspector of the Public Security Bureau, and Xu Yunliang, Xu Jianlong, and Li Rongbao were involved in an attempted kidnapping of Tan Nanshan's son in Changshou. After repeated interrogations and confrontations, the County Government has concluded the case. Now the county has received an order from the province to transfer Li and the other three to Suzhou for investigation. The case files are currently being reviewed and sent.

Zhouzhuang Robbery: The home of Dr. Zhao Linsheng in Niuli Village, east wall of Zhouzhuang, was robbed by more than ten bandits the night before, with a loss of more than 200 yuan.

Reorganization of the First District Office: Xing Songwen, the acting head of the First District Office, was arrested and detained the other day by order of the provincial government due to a certain case. Li County Magistrate ordered Assistant Xing Xiaoqing to transfer the district affairs to the district chief, Zhu Shuyun, who was selected by the hand order. The entire team was reorganized, and Cui Xilin, the district political inspector, was appointed as the instructor, and Shen was selected by the hand order as the assistant.

Danyang 80

Rampant Banditry in the Southwest Countryside: Large gangs of bandits, totaling more than 500, have been reported in the Pu District, bordering Danyang and Zhenjiang. The bandit leader, Chen Wenqi, is known for looting, arson, and murder. The village was suddenly surrounded by bandits, who set fire to the village, at dawn yesterday. The whole village was robbed, and many men and women were kidnapped. Fengluo Village in this county, which is very close, is experiencing a mass exodus of farmers who do not dare to live in peace. It is now reported that another gang of bandits is wreaking havoc in Naxiang Jiuli and other places. The County Government reported it and dispatched a police team to launch a swift counter-insurgency.

Police Arrest for Smoking, Resulting in a Fatality: Chen, the director of the First Public Security Bureau, was informed that Sun Chaoyu, a farmer in Shangzhuang Village, was privately smoking opium at home. He dispatched Patrol Chief Chen, leading armed police officers, to arrest him. Sun was in the act of smoking, and witnesses were obtained. He became overwhelmed with anger and emotion, and his long-standing illness was triggered, causing him to suddenly faint. His family, seeing this, shouted outside, attracting the villagers, who tied up the patrol chief and escorted him to the Fourth District Office. District Chief Hong considered the case to be significant and has transferred it to the County Government for interrogation.

Zhenjiang 81

Rampant Banditry in Baoyan in the Southern Countryside: Baoyan Town in the southern countryside of Zhenjiang, located at the intersection of Danyang, Jurong, and Zhenjiang, has flourishing commerce and prosperous residents. Jin Futian and Zhao Jinzhang, the first and second squadron leaders of the county police team, command two teams of soldiers stationed in the town to provide security. On the 7th of this month, the two teams were ordered to join the Baoyan Chamber of Commerce to suppress bandits in Baitou, more than ten miles away from the Zhenjiang Jurong border. It is reported that the bandits totaled about 300 people, secretly lurking in the Gaoli Mountain area of Jurong, were subordinates of Ma Yuren, were fully armed, and carried some kind of reactionary flag. The march set off at 9:00 AM. The police and militia numbered about 100. Unexpectedly, the police team encountered the bandits on the road in Xuxiang Village (three miles from Baitou). The police team panicked and fled, firing random shots into the sky along the way and discarding a large number of bullets along the way, as if they were resupplying the bandits. The residents of Xuxiang Village, seeing this, were terrified and fled with their families, their cries echoing through the fields. The militia, which fought valiantly in the front line, was eventually defeated due to the disparity in numbers. Five militiamen were injured in the battle, one died, and one was kidnapped. After seeing the police team retreat, the bandits acted with impunity, burning more than 1,000 houses in Baitou Town, Luxi, Dingjiayang, and other villages within a few miles, kidnapping dozens of residents, and injuring dozens of people. By noon at about 12:00, the entire police team had retreated to Baoyan, but not a single bullet remained. The merchants and residents of the town immediately gathered with Xie, the district chief of the Sixth District, to discuss plans for self-preservation. They planned to invite the two captains, Jin and Zhao, to attend, but all the captains and police had disappeared. The merchants and residents were both afraid and angry at the situation, and local order was almost disrupted. Fortunately, Zhang Guoquan, the deputy commander of the Self-Defense Corps, led more than 50 militiamen to join the Chamber of Commerce for defense and temporary relief. A representative was sent to the province to appeal for help, and Battalion Commander Wang of the Third Battalion of the Thirty-first Regiment of the Seventeenth Brigade of the Sixth Division led a team to suppress the bandits overnight and has now arrived at the town.

Prevention and Suppression.

Yangzhou 82

The Ministry of Communications' Reply Regarding Opposition to Telephone Rate Increases: Because telephone rates in Yangzhou have been repeatedly increased, telephone subscribers believe it is unacceptable. Therefore, they unanimously opposed the Ministry of Communications' order to increase the rate by one yuan. The Chamber of Commerce then requested the Ministry of Communications to withdraw the order. The Chamber has now received a reply, stating that the order to slightly increase the telephone rent in each telephone bureau is intended to seek the survival of the telephone business and to gradually reorganize it. It is hoped that you will understand the difficulties of the times and inform the business community to comply. The request to cancel the monthly rent increase and refund the registration fee cannot be approved. It is hoped that you will comply, etc. It is now reported that the subscribers intend to take a second step to resist, but it is still unknown whether it will be effective.

The Hall's Order on the Requirement to Provide Compensation for the Pujji Ferry Disaster: In the case of the drowning of passengers on the Pujji ferry in Liuwei due to the riverbank collapse in this county last month, the County Government has requested compensation. The former is a natural disaster (referring to Pujji), and the latter is a man-made disaster (referring to Yuniu). The request to order the Pujji ferry to bear the compensation is difficult to approve, etc.

Nantong 83

Surrounding and Suppressing the Native Bandits in Tongru: Li Changjiang, the commander of the Provincial Security Regiment, led his troops to join the police teams and self-defense corps of Tongtai counties to concentrate in Huangqiao on the 5th and advance to suppress the bandit areas. The 800 men of the surrendered Li Jigen were used as the vanguard. On the 9th, the bandits in the Zhentao, Siyu, Jiuyu, and other districts bordering Tongru were divided into two groups for encirclement and suppression. The battle was fierce, and more than 50 bandits were killed, and more than 30 firearms were seized. Mai Yanbiao, the platoon leader of the Provincial Security Regiment, and many soldiers were injured. Li Mingyang, the director of the Security Office, rushed from Taixing to Nantong on the 8th to supervise the suppression.

County Funds Advanced for the Allowance of Wounded Soldiers Not Yet Approved for Reimbursement: The Nantong Thirty-first Rear Hospital's allowance for wounded soldiers was advanced by the County Funds Production Office in succession due to the slow supply. The amount is huge. The County Government submitted a report to the provincial office requesting that the advanced funds be used to offset the tax. It was ordered that the funds were borrowed by the temporary dean without authorization. The Funds Production Office should directly consult for reimbursement. The request is not approved.

Fundraising Measures for the District Self-Defense Corps: The Nantong County Self-Defense Committee held its third conference on the 9th and decided on fundraising measures for the Self-Defense Corps in each district: (A) Agriculture and commerce are equally divided in the Chengzha and the two districts. (B) In the remaining districts, the maximum limit is 70% agriculture and 30% commerce, and the minimum limit is 90% agriculture and 10% commerce. Each district will formulate its own regulations based on the township conditions. The District Self-Defense Committee will check the budget and the actual number, investigate the capital of merchants and the farmland of farmers, allocate the amount of silver to be borne by each household, solicit local public opinion, and submit it to the county for approval.

Huzhou 84

Large Gang of Bandits Coveting Huzhou City: More than 30 bandit boats were suddenly discovered near Luoshe Town on the border of Deqing County in Huzhou. The military and police of the town investigated and learned that there were 150 bandits, with six machine guns and eighty or ninety wooden-cased guns. The military authorities reported to the neighboring military and police agencies and wired the province to request troops to suppress the bandits. The Seventh Regiment of the Security Team stationed in Jiaxing heard the news and immediately dispatched a company of soldiers. The provincial government also sent an additional patrol team and two warships, all of which rushed to the area overnight to join the troops and launch a counter-insurgency. However, the bandits noticed first and immediately went elsewhere. A group of residents have suffered a false alarm.

Liu Jing Village Robbery Case: In Liujing Village, seven miles away from Hongxing Bridge in Xixiang, Huzhou, Yin Changshun, who farms for a living, was suddenly attacked by a dozen bandits armed with guns at about 10 p.m. the other day. They broke into the house and looted all the clothes and other items. Before leaving, they left a note asking for 1,500 yuan and indicating where to contact them.

Pinghu 85

Two Cloth Shops Close Down in Datong Bridge: The cloth shop business in Pingyi has been very developed in recent years. In Datong Bridge Town in the northern countryside, between Xinqi and Zhongqi, two new cloth shops were opened in the East Market and North Market a month or two ago. Both were branches of Zhongqi. The business was booming, and a lot of cloth was collected every day. For some reason, the two shops simultaneously stopped business on the 5th and closed down invisibly. However, the houses were not returned. It is said that the sales areas could not be sold due to banditry. However, countless unemployed female workers have been added to the city.

The Speedboat Almost Caused a Disaster: The small wheelship, named Changshun, operating on the Xinqi Pinghu line, took advantage of the large number of passengers. At 4 p.m. on the 7th, it returned from Pinghu to Xinqi, towing several water police boats. When it reached the Guangchen Port and turned, the ship's captain sped up and advanced, causing the towed boat to almost sink. The sailors and goods were dumped into the river. Fortunately, passing boats rescued the sailors and salvaged the goods, so no disaster occurred.

Gaoyou 86

The Rampant Banditry at the Intersection of Jiangsu and Anhui: The counties of Tianchang and Ganyi in Anhui Province have long been suffering from the bandit Jiang Guochang (also known as San Tiao Tui). Provincial troops have been dispatched to suppress them repeatedly, but to no avail. Now, Jiang and the bandits have led five or six hundred bandits to occupy the towns of Jiupu and Liantang in Ganyi County, burning, killing, looting, and kidnapping more than a hundred hostages. Recently, they attacked Gangcheng Town in Tianchang County. The town closed the Siwei Gate tightly, and the county defense forces and self-defense corps fought to the death to resist. However, the blockhouse outside the fort has been occupied by bandits, and they are now at a stalemate. The bandits have also dispatched a small force to Genglutang and Gaomiao, which are only twenty miles away from Yanjiaqiao and Jingou in Gaoyou County, causing the towns to panic. Yesterday, they reported to the County Government in alarm. The Guan Port detained the native cloth produced in Jiangyin and other counties, which has always been transported to various counties in northern Jiangsu for consumption. It has long been approved to be tax-free. The cloth merchants from Gaoyu, Bao, Xing, and Su recently purchased a large amount of native cloth in Jiangyin County. Unexpectedly, it was detained when it was transported through the Yangyou Port. The cloth merchants have requested their respective counties to negotiate with them. It is heard that the chambers of commerce of the counties have jointly requested the superiors to order the port to release the cloth.

Hangzhou 87

Jinyun's Order is Completely Restored: After Zhejiang Provincial Government received the news that Jinyun was harassed by bandits, in addition to ordering Captain Gan to send more troops to suppress the bandits, the entire Second Battalion of the Seventh Regiment was sent from Yongkang on the 3rd. Yesterday, the Provincial Government received a telegram from Gan Qingchi, the commander of the Fourth Regiment, stating that Zhao's Battalion has arrived in Jinyun, and the order in Jinyun City has been completely restored. All the bandits are gone. Zhao's Battalion is now meeting and dispatching to the four villages to put down the embers. It is also reported that the bandits who violated Zhejiang and Fujian have been defeated by the brave pursuit of the security team. Taishun and Jinyun have been recaptured one after another, and the Kuai County Government has been completely burned, causing huge losses. Yesterday, the Provincial Government received a telegram from Zheng Xi, the County Magistrate of Jinyun County, reporting the losses of the financial department, stating that the county magistrate checked the items in the government after returning to the city and found that all of them were burned. Regarding the financial part, the losses were more than 2,300 yuan in regular tax, 940 yuan in central bonds and interest stored in the exchange, more than 15,000 yuan in various public debt tickets for postwar debt repayment, streamlining tariff, 35 relief, and more than 1,100 yuan in judicial income guarantee money. There were only more than 800 yuan in printed paper. The county magistrate, Zheng Xi, has failed to perform his duties and deserves to be punished. He has sent another telegram to request punishment. He will continue to report the loss of stored items after investigation. This telegram is respectfully submitted.

Please review and approve Zheng Xi, the County Magistrate of Jinyun County.

Ningbo 88

Yongning Ship Robbed: Yongning Ship from the Jiangbei Yongan Ningbo Ship Bureau in this port. At 9 a.m. on the 6th of this month, it set sail for Wenzhou, loaded with five or six hundred pieces of cargo such as tobacco leaves and two or three hundred passengers. The next day, it passed through Haimen. Some of the goods were loaded and unloaded, and some of the passengers got on and off. However, most of them were going to Haimen, so only a hundred or so people were left when it departed from Haimen. At about 11 p.m., it arrived at Shixing (more than 100 miles from Haimen) and was suddenly robbed by bandits. Twenty passengers were kidnapped, and all the luggage on the ship was robbed. Fortunately, the cargo in the lower cabin was not touched, and all seventy or so crew members were safe. After the bandits left, the ship returned to Haimen and reported to the general bureau. The command headquarters for suppressing bandits in the four subordinate ports of this port ordered a pursuit. The ship has returned to Wenzhou.

Village Council Conducts City-Building Issues: The city's village committees have been brewing a case for building a city for a long time. Yesterday, the village's joint communication office held a joint meeting and the following important resolutions were recorded (1) Not Recognize The Pricing Review Committee of City Organization Housing (1) Formulate an aggressive plan to develop the city, (1) dispatch personnel to thoroughly investigate raising donation fund distribution for old floating bridge construction.

Education News Headlines

Ministry of Education Explains Qualifications for Bureau Chiefs and Middle School Principals 89

The Ministry of Education, based on the request from Jia Huaiyu, the principal of the Quan Jiao County-level middle school in Anhui Province, for an explanation on whether graduates from schools such as fisheries can be selected and appointed as county education bureau chiefs and middle school principals, recently issued an instruction stating: "Received and understood. Upon investigation, schools of fisheries, accounting, textiles, etc., that enroll graduates from senior high schools or equivalent schools should be referred to as specialized schools. This is clearly stipulated in the regulations for specialized schools promulgated by this Ministry. Furthermore, the Department of Education of Anhui Province previously established the organizational regulations for county education bureaus in Anhui Province and the provisional regulations for the appointment, dismissal, and treatment of middle school principals in Anhui Province, which were submitted to the former University Council for approval and record. According to Article 7, Item 4 of the regulations, 'Those who have graduated from specialized schools or higher and have served in educational positions for three years or more are qualified to be county education bureau chiefs.' Also, Article 2, Clause A, Item 1 of the provisional regulations states, 'Graduates of specialized schools who have served in middle schools or higher or have managed educational administration for three years or more and have demonstrated outstanding performance are qualified to be fully accredited middle school principals.' You are hereby informed accordingly."

Zhejiang Education Commissioner Chen Reports Reason for Resignation 90

Due to Illness, It is Truly Difficult to Endure, Seeking Resignation Urgently

Endeavoring to Serve as Usual, Hoping All Colleagues

Will Strive to Handle Matters Expeditiously and Conclude the Education Department's Memorial Week in Front of Sun Yat-sen at 8:30 AM the Day Before Yesterday, Commissioner Chen Braved Illness to Arrive at the Office, Leading All Staff to Attend, Performing the Ceremony as Usual. His political report, in addition to outlining military and political matters, also briefly mentioned his personal resignation, stating: "My physical health has always been weak, and I suffer from heart disease. I have repeatedly wanted to retire to recuperate. In the past two months, various illnesses have arisen, and my condition has worsened. Last week, my teeth and gums swelled and ached, preventing me from sleeping at night. Medical diagnoses all indicate that unless I completely withdraw from everything and have at least six months of absolute rest, my illness will become incurable. Under these circumstances, if I continue to force myself to work, my illness will inevitably hinder my duties, which would be detrimental to both the public and private spheres. While we serve the Party and the nation, we should not consider personal interests, but we should also only take on duties that our bodies can handle without hindering our work. Otherwise, the crime of neglecting public duties cannot be avoided. Therefore, I have already submitted my resignation from all my concurrent positions to the provincial government and the central government some days ago. Although I have not yet received approval from the central government, my physical condition is such that my desire to leave is extremely urgent. I will do everything I can to seek understanding from all parties to fulfill my initial desire to recuperate. During this waiting period, I must come to the office despite my illness due to my responsibilities. My colleagues have worked together for more than a year, and they should understand the difference between an individual and an organization. We are here to serve education and to serve Zhejiang. Do not allow my words to cause any slackening in your work. You should continue to be proactive and responsible as usual. For all matters handled by each person, strive for speed. Any accumulated items should be cleared quickly. Always be prepared to conclude matters at any time. This is what I have often cautioned in the past. The difference between a new organization and an old government office lies in this. I may need to reduce my time in the office due to my health. I hope that all colleagues will always encourage each other with what I have said today."

Local News

Ministry of Education Commends Shanghai Education Bureau 93

For Compiling Supplementary Readers for Lower Grades of Elementary School

The Shanghai Education Bureau previously submitted to the Ministry of Education that, in order for elementary school children to understand the significance of National Revolution Commemorative holidays, they should be provided with supplementary readers. In the past, such teaching materials were temporarily selected by the class teachers of each school, and it goes without saying that the ideas could not be consistent and the content could not be appropriate. Recognizing this, the bureau specifically assigned personnel to compile ten types of supplementary readers for the revolutionary commemorative holidays suitable for elementary school children in the lower grades, which were divided into ten volumes and are planned to be released soon. The original text is hereby submitted for inspection and approval, and instructions should be issued swiftly for compliance. The Ministry of Education recently instructed the bureau: "The submitted documents and attachments have been fully received and understood. All the submitted books have now been reviewed and completed by the Ministry. The review shows that the content and materials are adapted to the needs of children and the illustrations are precise. It is evident that the bureau knows how to make efforts and research in guiding the work of schools, which is deeply commendable. However, there are still some inappropriate words in the books. You should revise them according to the comments before being allowed to publish them and use them as supplementary readers for children in the lower grades of elementary schools. You may also publish the words 'Approved for publication after review by the Ministry of Education' on the books. When the books are printed, the format should be suitable for children's psychology, and the illustrations should be reproduced without distortion. Two copies of the published books should be sent to the Ministry for record. Furthermore, supplementary readers for elementary schools have a great function in teaching and have the same value as textbooks. Although there are many published ones on the market, there are still not many suitable ones. During the period of the provisional standards for elementary school curriculum, each school should use the practical experiment results to compile reading materials. There should also be no lack of good books. You should immediately transfer the order to the schools under your jurisdiction to collect them at any time, and submit them to the bureau for detailed review before selecting the best ones to be sent to the Ministry for review and reply for compliance."

Saying a Word for the South-Bound Football Teams: Hu Wenhu 102

Teams Must Cooperate... Hosted by the National Sports Advancement Association

(August 30th, Singapore Correspondence) In the recent two months, well-known domestic football teams, such as the China Expedition Football Team, South China, and China have come to Singapore one after another. The overseas Chinese, out of patriotic ideals, have warmly welcomed them, and Mr. Hu Wenhu, the owner of Yong An Tang in Singapore, has done his best as the host. Mr. Hu's enthusiasm for promoting sports is rare both at home and abroad. However, Mr. Hu, in view of the fact that the visiting teams cannot concentrate talents, resulting in their strength not being strong enough, deeply regrets this and has written "Saying a Word for the South-Bound Football Teams" to advise the teams and hope that the National Sports Advancement Association will rise up to host the event, which will have a multiplier effect. The original text of Mr. Hu is recorded below: "This time, the South China, Lehua (i.e., China Expedition Football Team), and China football teams have come to the south one after another. The team members themselves have gained the benefit of observing artistic soil, and the South China sports community has been given an intangible incentive to promote it. Most of our fathers and brothers have also been able to enjoy the limited blessing of appreciating the artistic performances of the athletes, which is a great event. However, although the skills of the three teams of athletes are generally good, the advantages of offense and defense must have their own strengths and weaknesses, and they are not perfect. Therefore, they win often, but sometimes they are inevitably calculated by the opposing team, which is a pity. A football team on an expedition to a foreign country, under the gaze of China and foreign countries, although the way to win or lose is small, the glory of the national system is at stake. We firmly believe that combining the athletes of the three Hua teams into a strong team will not only run rampant in the South China Sea, but can also be invincible and unconquerable. Even on an expedition to Europe and the United States, competing with the blue-eyed and purple-bearded people, they may not give way much. However, their forces are weak when divided. Team A is good at attacking, but the rear is empty. When enemy soldiers knock on the door, they open the door and invite thieves. Team B has a strong defense, but the front line is too weak. Those who cannot fight are not easy to defend. The attack and defense of the two teams have their own strengths, but the whole team occasionally has weaknesses. Sometimes, moving one hair will move the whole body. On the day of the ball war, the army is not harmonious. The whole audience is silent and drooping. The spectators on the wall feel the same way. Each team of athletes, being in the game, must have the feeling of after the fierce feeling."

"I think that in the future, football teams should be hosted by the National Sports Association when going on expeditions. Select the elite to form an iron army. An expedition to the South China Sea, once a year, will see the division to where it is, destroying the rotten and breaking the pine, raising the prestige of the Han people and snowing the nickname of the sick man. The glory of the sports world is also the happiness of all the overseas Chinese."

"Some say that each team has its own history of organization, and the separation of ways is different, and cooperation is difficult. I don't know that things are divided into private and public, internal and external, and the boundaries should be strict. Moreover, sports is a noble industry, and athletes should have a broad and great spirit. How can we misrepresent meaningless prejudices and create divisions to hinder the development of the sports industry and affect the glory of the national system? I hope that the athletes of the three teams will think about it carefully."

Local News

China National Aviation Corporation to Conduct Test Flight to Chongqing Tomorrow Morning 109

Official Flights Scheduled to Begin Early Next Month

According to a new contract signed on July 1st, China National Aviation Corporation was reorganized and merged with the existing Shanghai-Chengdu Aviation Corporation to become a commercial aviation transport company. China National Aviation Corporation originally had four aircraft, all of the Loening type. Shanghai-Chengdu Aviation Corporation initially had nine aircraft, all of the Stinson type, but two were later transferred to the General Headquarters, and three more were borrowed. Therefore, when merged with China National Aviation Corporation, only three remained. China National Aviation Corporation recently ordered another Loening amphibious aircraft from the United States, which will arrive in Shanghai on the 19th of this month. The company's Shanghai-Hankou air transport service has been running for nearly a year, and its success in mail delivery and passenger transport is widely known. Recently, the company has been actively expanding its routes to the interior of Sichuan. A plane has been scheduled to fly to Chongqing for a test flight tomorrow morning, along with a survey of the Yangtze River. It has also been decided to start official flights early next month. The flight from Shanghai to Hankou will take seven hours, with an overnight stay in Hankou. From Hankou to Chongqing, it will take eight hours. Thus, a journey from Shanghai to Chongqing, which previously took no less than two weeks, can now be completed in two days, greatly benefiting merchants and travelers. This also marks a significant achievement in China's aviation transportation industry.

Preparations The company has already sent personnel to Yichang and Chongqing to prepare for the extended routes, including liaising with local authorities, installing buoys on the river surface, arranging fuel supplies, and weather reports. All preparations have been completed. Several wireless radio sets have been shipped from Shanghai for installation at various stops. The existing Shanghai-Hankou route uses American Loening amphibious aircraft, as they can land on the river at any time, making them the most reliable aircraft for the Yangtze River route. However, the upper reaches of the Yangtze River have steep mountains and turbulent rapids. The first test flight is expected to be challenging. However, the company is using the latest amphibious aircraft, which can land on both land and water when necessary, mitigating potential dangers. The test flight from Shanghai to Chongqing is scheduled for tomorrow morning at 8:00 AM. The plane will stay overnight in Hankou, then proceed to Yichang the next day, Wanzhou the third day, and arrive in Chongqing on the fourth day, allowing for detailed surveying of the terrain and arrangement of parking facilities. The return journey will be a direct flight from Chongqing back to Hankou for an overnight stay, and then back to Shanghai the next day. The total distance from Shanghai to Chongqing is over 1,200 miles, requiring only twelve hours of non-stop flying. After the successful test flight, official flights will begin within a month, with stops planned in Yichang and Wanzhou to load and unload mail and passengers. The new aircraft arriving on the 19th of this month will be used for flights between Hankou and Chongqing. Initially, there will be only one flight per week between Hankou and Chongqing. After the official flight between Shanghai and Chongqing is successful, plans will continue to extend the route to Chengdu. The test flight will be piloted by the company's Chief and Deputy Chief of Aviation, American Mr. Smith and Mr. Nie Kaiyi. Mr. Smith has many years of flying experience in the United States. Mr. Nie is a graduate of an American aviation school and has many years of experience in the Chinese aviation industry. He was also involved in the establishment of Shanghai-Chengdu Aviation Corporation under the Ministry of Communications. The company's Vice Chairman, Mr. Hamilton, will also be on board.
