A Laughing Matter 134

— Hai Ke

Guest (knocking on the door of a small house and asking a young man who has been married for more than a year)—Sir, are you the master of this house?

Young man—No. The master of this house is sleeping peacefully in the cradle. He is the authority of the family. You only need to ask my wife to know.

Child (sitting on the tram, staring blankly at a large, fat man sitting opposite him)—Hee hee hee.

Fat man—Why are you staring at my face all the time? What are you doing?

Child—I want to look at the streets outside the window, but you are completely blocking them. I can't see anything, so I have to look at you.

Old maid (teasing a child)—Child, how old are you this year?

Child—Five years old.

Old maid—Guess how old I am.

Child—One, two, three, four... I can only count to forty. I can't count any higher than that.

A—I'm sorry, I'm not going to buy your old car.

B—Why?

A—Because the doctor said my health is good. I should walk more every day.

B—That doesn't matter. If you sit in my car, I guarantee you won't be able to drive very far before you have to get out and walk.

The Achievements of the National Army Amidst the Sounds of War 135

— Qing Song Jushi

A certain Mr. Yu, a friend of mine, has been serving in the Central Army for many years. He is intelligent and brave, deep and resolute, and decisive in his work. This time, in the campaign to suppress Yan and Feng, he was promoted by the Central Government and appointed as a battlefield inspector. He traveled tirelessly on the Longhai and Jinpu railways, breaking through strongholds and overcoming obstacles. He participated in every battle. Recently, due to the initial stabilization of military affairs, he returned home for a brief rest. After years of separation, we met with joy. According to his description of the situation on the front lines, Generalissimo Chiang's use of troops is like a god, clear in his assessment of the enemy. He knows that war cannot be fought with force, but must be assessed according to the situation and seize the key points. Battles cannot be fought with recklessness, but must be approached with deep thought and observation of changes. Wherever the army goes, it digs deep trenches and builds high ramparts. In addition to densely woven electric fences, branches are piled up to form mountain ridges, so high that they cannot be climbed. They are extremely strong, creating a situation where one man can hold the pass against ten thousand men. In their battle formations, guns, cannons, knives, and spears are divided into teams and interspersed with each other in a methodical and infinitely variable manner. For example, if we divide our forces and try to surround them, then each tunnel and each sentry post will resist separately, combining long and short weapons, and responding to the unusual with the ordinary. They are worthy of being called a disciplined army. In addition, they love and care for their soldiers, and encourage the three armies. The commanders move after careful planning, are brave and know their direction. The machine guns are fierce and unstoppable, and the air force takes advantage of weaknesses. The soldiers are well-fed and the horses are vigorous, and they have righteousness and confidence. However, Yan and Feng are self-willed and poor at assessing people. They have little food and insufficient weapons and ammunition, yet they want to compete with our army. It is clear that they do not know their own limitations. I once heard that Feng was good at attacking and Yan was good at defending. Yan clearly knew this but deliberately violated it. He also made a desperate gamble, using the large knife units to attack and storm fortifications on the Longhai Railway. Day after day, he drove bodies of flesh and blood into the fierce heat of the sun and the power of artillery fire. Although the northwestern warriors are skilled, their brute force and fierce attacks have resulted in heavy casualties and a loss of morale. Although our army has suffered some damage, it is no more than a drop in the bucket. Yan's army occupied Jinan, relying on its fortifications for several days. Its military strength cannot be said to be weak. However, the central palace was not defended, losing the advantage of a commanding position. They had no preparation for rain gear or drainage, and were careless and negligent. Both of these are fatal injuries. Our army is mostly from Guangdong, and is good at swimming and fighting. They thought that if they missed this opportunity, heaven would strike their army. They clenched their fists and rubbed their palms, and advanced together. Above, airplanes dropped bombs. Below, machine guns swept across. Yan's army suspected that the Flying General had descended from the sky. Even if they wanted to fight a battle against the city, they had already been defeated and scattered. They fled in panic across the river. This shows that the two men only have empty reputations, and are not as good as our army, whose attack and defense are coordinated and appropriate.

President Chiang's Passion for Painting 136

— Tang Bi Hua

President Chiang, who has worked hard and achieved great merit, is fond of calligraphy and painting, especially landscapes. Recently, because the scenic spot of Xuedou in Fenghua is the best in all of Zhejiang, it is a pity that there are no famous painters to take a true picture of it, which he deeply regrets. There is a certain Shi Hou, a Buddhist monk, who was born into a prominent family but has escaped into the Buddhist faith. He is good at painting landscapes and his name is highly regarded for a time. Those who obtain his paintings cherish them as if they were the most precious jade. When this matter was reported to Chiang, he was asked to go to Fenghua to take real pictures on the spot. Shi Hou went as ordered and painted a draft of forty paintings. The layers of green are stacked upon each other and the scenery is excellent. It is worthy of being a famous scenic area. The other day, I visited Shi Hou at the Shanghai South Water Immortal Palace. He showed me unfinished drawings. The brushstrokes were old and powerful, which was admirable. I expect that when the paintings are completed, they will be famous and valuable. President Chiang's concern for his hometown and his passion for painting are truly commendable. I have written this down.

Funeral for Mrs. Qian Shoutie 137

— Yanzi

Ms. Han Buyi from Yun Jian, named Xiu, was skilled in painting and proficient in Han clerical script. Three years ago, her sister's husband, Sun Xuenie, acted as matchmaker, and she married Qian Shoutie, a renowned figure in epigraphy, calligraphy, and painting. They were inseparable and deeply in love. Recently, she suddenly passed away from a lung ailment, much to the regret of those who knew her. On the sixth of this month, a memorial service was held at Chongfa Temple on Guling Road. Numerous figures from the literary and artistic circles attended. The plaster statue provided at the service was a gift from Jiang Xiaojian, exuding grace and a lifelike resemblance. Prominent painters such as Hashimoto Kansetsu from Japan all sent large floral wreaths. The elegiac couplets were exquisite beyond description. Here, I selectively record some of the most remarkable ones. Wang Yiting's couplet read: "Du Lanxiang departed long ago, leaving behind jade slips; Lü E'hua arrives without a fixed abode, a mere fantasy of golden rings." Yu Youren's couplet read: "Three years of shared hearts, graced by gentle breezes in the evening; Six months of lung ailment, dew foreshadowing autumn." Sun Xuenie's couplet read: "The official document sealed a good match, marrying her to Zhou Lang; The Jiangzu region praised her as a female scholar, her epitaph becoming her final work; Devastated, like Xun Ling, I see no Lady Guan in the hall." The wording was appropriate and the double entendres clever. However, the one that most impressed this reporter was Xie Jinyu from Wujin: "Jade pendants are lost in the heavens, hastily departing from the feast; A crane's back carries a short dream on the celestial wind; The spiritual herbs of Huangshan are exhausted, the painting scrolls remaining; The dragon palace pillows cause the autumn waves to grieve." Exquisitely beautiful, every word carefully chosen, truly deserving of first place. My old friend Ren Jinshu's couplet read: "A precious couple entrusted to ephemeral existence, her small portrait engraved in my heart; A fragile body, thinner than an autumn swallow; A love that sealed a vow in heaven; Paintings wounding the soul, dark dust obscuring the night cicada." Combining sorrow and beauty. Others, such as Huang Taixuan's couplet, read: "Three years achieved success swiftly, excelling in painting and calligraphy, truly a talented woman; Two marriages still seeking milk, fragmented silk and remnant paper, leaving sorrow to old friends." The wording was poignant, offering a fresh perspective. He Tianjian's couplet read: "Meeting in autumn on the sea, how can one bear to be like Pan Qi from Jiannan; Transforming into a crane in Yun Jian, her previous life must have been Du Lanxiang." The lines were also detached and transcendent. The rest are difficult to recall. Upon returning, I take up my pen to record them.

After Watching "Wang Zhaojun" 138

— A Wanderer on the Edge of the World

The Xi Society's opera department's first performance of "Wang Zhaojun" took place at the New Oriental Theater near Yokobashi on North Sichuan Road. Having been invited by Gui Gongchuang, a staff member of the society, I attended the performance on the evening of September 4th around 7 p.m. I have much to record from what I saw.

The main character in the play is Ms. Li Lilian, who played Zhaojun. According to someone, she is very emotional, so her performance was extremely sad and delicate. In the third act, Zhaojun sang a solo, which Ms. Li performed in the "Cantonese Ballad" style, her voice clear and bright, evoking a sense of Lingnan folk songs and inspiring an aesthetic appreciation. Mr. Zhang Junxie, who played Emperor Yuan, wore ancient costumes and sang in a European style. As Mr. Zhu Yingpeng said on the first page of the script, "Although drama expresses life, it also has spatial and temporal aspects. What it expresses should be a response to the times. 'New wine in old bottles' may seem somewhat comical, but it actually contains something truly new." He also said, "Meaningful new dramas can draw on ancient themes, but ancient dramas should be given a new interpretation and imbued with a new life." In this light, Mr. Zhang's use of a Western style to sing about Han Dynasty events, perhaps, contained elements of new life? Furthermore, Ms. Hu Manqian, who played the palace maid, had a natural demeanor and clear articulation. Li Hua's Huhanxie and the four or five who played the foreign riders had makeup, expressions, and tones that were rough and boisterous, reminding one of the barbaric state of the Huns back then. Other roles, such as Mr. Zhou Juanhong's overly courteous censor and Mr. Huang Huang's doddering record keeper, as well as the several little girls who played the lively children of Chang'an, were all excellent. The actors being like this, the scenery and plot were also well-matched. What was most commendable was that the actors were Cantonese but spoke standard Mandarin fluently. This was the second day of the society's performance, and the results were already remarkable. It is said that it will continue until the end of the month, with a new program every ten days. In that case, it will undoubtedly become more polished and impressive. Gentlemen who love drama, why not go and see it for yourselves?

A Brief Account of Xixi 139

— Yingchuan Furun

Furun, a native of Xixi, would like to talk about the events of Xixi. I think that readers would be delighted to hear them.

Xixi is located outside Qiantang Gate in Hangzhou, starting from Songmu Chang and ending at Liuxia Town, flowing along the mountains for eighteen li. The water is clear and pure, and the scenery is exceptionally beautiful. Whenever there is a moonlit night or a flowery morning, one can row a boat in Luhua Bay, where the reflection of the peaks is inverted, creating a constantly changing panorama, giving one a sense of being detached from the world.

In the past, there were many plum trees on both banks, with jade pressing against sandalwood. Spreading horizontally across the stream, the moonlight after snow was nothing but pictorial and poetic. Today, however, it is a small calamity of vicissitudes, with rows of elm and willow trees. The spring scenery of Jiangnan is outshone by Dengwei. "Exploring Plum Blossoms in Xixi" only occupies one spot among the ten scenic spots of Qiantang in name only.

In Anle Shanyang, there is Yongxing Temple, an ancient temple from the Tang Dynasty. The Song Dynasty Buddhist monk Jigong once stayed here. According to legend, a local who ate snails would cut off their tails. Jigong took pity on them and begged to throw them into the flowing water in front of the temple, and they all lived. Now, five hundred years later, the snails still exist. The four so-called great families of Xixi were Shen Banjie (house), Wang Shiwu (wealth), Ma Laoye (power), and Cen Mantang (sons). But now, the Shen house has changed hands, the Wang family has declined, the Cen descendants are not prosperous, and Ma Er died early. Human affairs are full of changes, in general.

Huawu is located on a non-mountain road, backed by Dingzi Lake. Surrounded by mountains, it contains a small stream. The sun-遮蔽 bamboos and pines, cold-hearted springs and stones. The thrush sings all day long. It is no less than a fairyland. Many eminent monks and men of letters lived here, whistling and singing. Green歙 swords and red fish provide much adornment. Tourists compare it to the Shanyin Road.

Internal Politics of Post-War Poland (IV) 140

— Li Liu Zeng, sent from Paris

Therefore, the initial goal of the French was to gradually unify the laws concerning public order and commercial activities. The first law promulgated and implemented throughout the country was a criminal procedure law, followed by several regulations on nationality and one on company bylaws. In addition, a decree was promulgated to amend the provisions on women's rights in the former Prussian region, because those restrictions on the abilities of married women conflicted with the laws in force in other parts of Poland. As for the remaining items, most of the several laws formerly in use were recognized as valid, but a new decree was enacted to resolve the legal disputes arising from the simultaneous existence of these various legal systems.

The provisional government has established a law codification committee, whose work is currently still in progress. The most difficult task is the compilation of civil law, the current difficulties being not only legal issues, but also many moral and political issues. Marriage regulations are one of the most difficult issues to resolve. In the future, will Polish law stipulate civil marriage or religious marriage? Will divorce be allowed, or absolutely forbidden? This serious issue has sparked heated debate in political circles. Some parliamentarians have proposed an interesting compromise, according to which civil marriages permitting divorce and religious marriages not permitting divorce would coexist. Those marrying could choose either form beforehand.

Due to limited space in this newspaper, the reporter cannot list all the difficulties in unifying Polish internal affairs and conduct more specialized research. However, from the above, it can be seen that the Polish government is striving for unity in both administration and justice amidst all difficulties. Although the current achievements are not entirely satisfactory, there are extenuating circumstances. Although the future is full of difficulties, the government's work is easier to carry out because of Poland's nationwide desire for internal unity.

Furthermore, whether Polish internal affairs can be unified is not only related to the interests of the Polish people. It also has a great impact on European peace. If Poland has only a unified name, but the judicial and administrative systems and other institutions in various parts of the country differ from each other, continuing the old habits of the partition era, then Poland will be in danger, as will European peace. Conversely, if Poland can be truly united and integrated as a whole, then its national power will increase day by day, and it can become a buffer zone for the powers of Central Europe, which has no small relationship with the prospects for peace.

Warmth in the Heart (274) 141

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboos and Mottled Doors, Her Heart Breaks; Red Lotus Fragrance Fades, a Daughter Departs from Home

Because of this impression, Cuiyun thought that the Ningbo old woman was so frightening, and she couldn't help but turn pale at the mention of Ningbo people, thinking that all Ningbo women were tigresses. In reality, this is not entirely true. Their men have a kind of daring nature, and of course the women also have this courage to dare to act. Although Cuiyun felt that Zhang Yiqing was a bit older, he was still alright. She was just afraid of the Ningbo old woman's power, and couldn't help but hesitate a bit. However, Zhang Yiqing repeatedly requested, and even knelt down to beg her to agree. Cuiyun also asked his close friends, who often came with him, for details. None of what Zhang Yiqing said was a lie. He did have a wife living in the countryside of Ningbo, who had never been to Shanghai. Zhang Yiqing did go back to Ningbo once a year, and sometimes didn't even go back once. This wife could be considered as if she didn't exist. Other than happily sending some money back to the countryside, there seemed to be no relationship at all. That friend also told her that Zhang Yiqing's old woman was a completely crude and ugly country woman, who could only be a rough servant compared to you, Miss Three. Cuiyun said, "We can't say that. As the saying goes, the one who enters the door first is the elder for three days. No matter what, she's always the '横闊豎', and I'm always the '七大八'." That friend said, "Our Brother Yiqing is naturally satisfied to have someone like you, Miss Three. And you don't go to Ningbo, you live in Shanghai. Who wouldn't call you Tai?" Cuiyun also inquired about Zhang Yiqing's background from his friend. According to that friend, Zhang Yiqing had suffered a lot since he was a child. When he first came to Shanghai, he apprenticed in a small money shop, and even had to empty the master's chamber pot. But he was very hardworking. Because one of his uncles worked as an old secretary in a money house on Houmalu, he relied on his uncle's influence to be recommended to this business. If he quit, no one would be able to recommend him. Later, because he was hardworking and capable, he rose to this position. How could someone without real skills reach this position? Now, in the Shanghai business community, he can be considered someone. Foreigners also trust him. That's really not easy." These friends were all on Zhang Yiqing's side. They were all so-called hangers-on, following his reins every day, running errands for him. Where would there be any truth? They just blew and flattered him. Cuiyun believed it to be true, thinking that she had consulted widely and that her friends were all of one voice, so of course it was reliable. Since the Ningbo old woman was in the countryside, she wouldn't come to Shanghai. In Shanghai, she would naturally be the only one in charge. Added to this was Zhang Yiqing's charm and smooth talk, as well as his lavish displays. In just a few days, Cuiyun agreed to marry him. She thought that she would escape the pit of fire and embark on the road to happiness, finally finding a place to belong to her body.

Cotton Yarn Market Struggles to Gain Momentum 147

The yarn market fell in the morning but rose in the afternoon, but the overall trend remained sluggish. This was mainly due to the slow sales of spot yarn and the increasingly subdued overseas cotton yarn market, leading to a generally bearish sentiment. However, some manufacturers remained firm, increasing their buying pressure. As for the Chaozhou traders, they viewed the ongoing war as never-ending, and their determination to sell off their accumulated inventory became even stronger. The competition between bulls and bears was particularly intense.

The human brand yarn market was weak in the morning but slightly improved in the evening. The market opened weakly due to poor environmental conditions and a further decline in the price of third-grade yarn. Sellers increased, and market sentiment was weak, with prices falling by five to six qian. The second and third sessions remained soft, with distant contracts falling by eight to nine qian and near contracts falling by one to two qian. The afternoon yarn market was relatively stable, but the market tightened slightly due to some buying activity, with prices rising by one, four, and six qian. Grain: New Western Japonica Rice Initially Shows Stability 150

Few Arrivals at Zhabei Yesterday, few ships arrived at the river, and sales were quiet in the street. The arrival of broken japonica rice from the northern gangs was scarce, and there were various related factors, so the source of supply was greatly affected. The Xieji Company, currently known as a free trading business, has been investigated and approved by the Municipal Council, as reported in a certain newspaper, to not be held liable for past actions and to operate according to shipping regulations in the future. Therefore, rice merchants from the river who were dissatisfied with the evaluation of japonica rice have slightly increased the price per dan for sales to Xieji Company. The japonica rice of Xieji Company is evaluated according to quality and market price. Therefore, although the japonica rice market is scarce, the market is stable. More than forty stones of new Western japonica rice were seen yesterday, with a price of 19 yuan, and the market was stable. New Eastern japonica rice arriving from the river was very cheap, and sellers wanted to raise prices, but because buyers were dissatisfied, the market fluctuated around 17.5 yuan, and the trend remained flat. New sharp-pointed rice initially wanted to rise, but still opened at 15.5 yuan in Hangzhou. New guest sharp-pointed rice remained around 14 yuan, and the situation turned firm. White Yuan continued to show stability, which was due to both arrivals and sales.

Few Arrivals from South Shanghai, Market Sales are Quite Sluggish. The stock of Northern japonica rice is scarce, and the source of arrivals from the lake is still declining. Although medium-quality goods appeared weak, they stabilized in the afternoon, which was due to the small amount of goods. The buying interest for thin paper rice from the southern gangs was normal. This was also due to the impact of low inventory levels, so the above market will be on par with the Zhabei market. The price of new Eastern japonica rice opened at 17.5 yuan, and the market was also unchanged. New sharp-pointed rice and Yuan rice were all stable. The stock of each store was insufficient, and the intention to purchase was quite active, so the buyers in both the north and south markets were very refreshed.

Guest Xian Rice Arrivals Decrease, Prices Rise 151

Hunan Rice Being Handled by Tianjin Gang. Yesterday, the market conditions for foreign guest xian rice turned firm. Because the source of supply from Hunan and Jiangxi suddenly decreased, everyone was bullish on the market. However, there were still no large purchases by guest gangs, so the price increase was not fully realized. As a result, only Hunan rice rose by nearly one jiao, because more than 300 bags of Hunan rice were handled by the Tianjin gang. The mentality of the cargo owners became more firm. Jiangxi rice was only handled by local street and rural merchants, and only showed a slight increase of two or three points. The entire market was slightly active due to low inventory levels, and transactions were also small. A total of 800 bags of Hunan Jing were opened at a price of 12.4 yuan to 11.8 yuan, 600 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled early rice at a price of 13.2 yuan to 11.7 yuan, and 100 bags of machine-milled late rice at a price of 14.4 yuan. Only 100 bags of foreign rice were opened, with the large twist at a price of 12.15 yuan. Except for the 300 bags of Hunan rice purchased by the Tianjin gang, all were purchased by local street and rural merchants.

Flour Market Falls Sharply 152

Foreign Wheat Continues to Fall Slightly. Factories Start to Sell Futures. Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, prices for all months gradually fell sharply. Because the price of foreign wheat fell by another four or five jiao, external participants felt uneasy. Factories still maintained buying pressure on the near-term and did not loosen their grip, but they had already begun to sell off the distant months, because foreign flour wheat has gradually entered the market, and factories seem to be cutting off their own lifeline if they continue to squeeze. The price of foreign flour yesterday was lower than the previous week. The price of domestic flour was only 3.75 yuan, and no one was asking about it. Because prices were falling, it was difficult to guarantee that they would not fall again in the future, so everyone was watching. However, with this comparison to foreign countries, the market mentality became softer and softer, so the decline in the distant term reached three fen, and the future seemed to be in a precarious state. As a result, the current month fell by 1.75 fen compared to the previous day, October fell by 2.25 fen, November fell by 2.75 fen, December/January fell by three fen, and February fell by 2.75 fen.

Wheat Futures Plunge by Six to Seven Fen 153

Spot Factories Do Not Open... Instead Sell Standards. Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, prices for all months consistently plunged. Because the near-term months saw that the manufacturers were forced to lower prices for spot wheat, the prices of foreign wheat in the distant months continued to fall, and the manufacturers were also selling large quantities of hedged wheat for December and later. This type of action may be because foreign wheat has become fixed, and to protect their interests, they sold standard wheat. In this situation, the external bulls felt that there was no way to resist any longer. As a result, the current month fell by seven fen compared to the previous day, October/November fell by five fen, December fell by seven fen, January fell by six fen, and February fell by seven fen. The spot wheat market remained extremely quiet. Only 292 bags of Xuzhou wheat were opened throughout the day at a price of 4.85 taels, which was about one qian lower than the beginning of the week.

Standard Dalian Soybeans Plunge by One Qian 154

Yesterday, the Dalian soybean December futures market fell sharply. The production market telegraphed continuous declines, and the Fengqi of the traders was particularly smooth. According to the stable harvest in eastern provinces this year, the intention of merchants to sell was strong, so prices fell back continuously. Yesterday, it fell by as much as 1.2 fen, and the closing price was only 5.25 taels, which is a rare occurrence in the market.

Shanghai Market

Business News 181

The Henmao Automobile Company announces that "Free Wheeling" is the Stude­baker factory's unprecedented advancement in automobile engine construction. With this feature, the car's driving speed is faster than the engine's rotation. Yesterday, our company displayed this new car at our new showroom at 23 Metcalfe Road, holding the first trial run ever seen in the Far East. The audience was amazed and envious, praising it highly. This new invention contains the ultimate in mechanical engineering principles and is the result of the exhaustive efforts and meticulous research of the Stude­baker factory's leading engineering experts. It is unprecedented and truly remarkable. This feature is available on the Stude­baker President and Commander eight-cylinder new cars. The various advantages are unmatched, and it is not only about making driving more comfortable. "Free Wheeling" means that no matter the vehicle's speed, gears can be shifted at will without using the clutch. The clutch is only needed for the initial start. Once the foot is removed from the accelerator, the engine immediately drops to idling speed, greatly saving gasoline and oil. Notably, ordinary cars consume more gasoline and oil when traffic is congested. However, "Free Wheeling" uniquely saves 12% of gasoline and 20% of oil. As for tires, rear axles, connecting rods, clutches, gearboxes, and other parts that are normally subject to wear and tear, this can be avoided, reducing carbon buildup inside the engine. The car's driving is extremely quiet and safer. The Stude­baker eight-cylinder automobile has been a leader in the automotive world for years, and this great invention is like adding flowers to embroidery. However, the factory's leading engineers are still not satisfied. The wheelbase is lengthened, the car body is enlarged, the effect is more significant, the action is more stable, and the style is more beautiful. As for horsepower, the President has increased from 115 to 122 horsepower, and the Commander has increased from 80 to 101 horsepower. The nine-bearing crankshaft is absolutely balanced, providing extreme smoothness. Other equipment, such as shock absorbers, mufflers, driving gears, as well as the springs, brakes, water tanks, and other parts, and the arrangement of car lights and car seats, are all perfect and extremely suitable. As for the advantages of strong and superior construction, low center of gravity, durability, and extreme comfort, they are renowned worldwide. Therefore, sales are brisk and warmly welcomed by people everywhere.

The Tongchunxiang Foreign Cloth Store at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Shilu Road announces that it has been in business for over 60 years and is the only old foreign cloth store on Nanjing Road. Now, to expand business, it is re-equipping and adding various floral silk velvet, wool serge, silk crepe, and other items. Therefore, starting today, it is holding a major sale for 25 days. The store's goods are indeed cheaper than market prices, resulting in unusually crowded customers.

The Shanghai Cherry Stamp Company announces that, to expand its business, it has moved to 323 Annakin Road and is operating as usual. Those who wish to obtain exquisite stamps from various countries, please include 50 cents in Chinese stamps and a large bag will be given away.

The Guanghua Bookstore on Fourth Ma Road announces that it has recently published 15 new books in one month. The authors and translators are all famous novelists or writers, so several books have been selected by schools in various provinces as textbooks, which are highly praised. Recently, to benefit readers, all books, both local and foreign editions, will be sold at reduced prices for 20 days, starting yesterday.

The Daguang Company at 9 Hankou Road announces that its manager, Mr. Song Zijiang, has recently invented an automatic copier with a delicate structure, flexible operation, and low price. It can be called a good product among domestic goods.

The Sanfeng Company at 20 Museum Road announces that since the company began manufacturing domestic athletic undershirts last year, many large stores in various provinces and this port have been purchasing from the company, such as Sincere, Wing On, Commercial Press, China General Agency, and more than ten others, which are all selling them. There are also distributors in Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Nanjing, Beijing, Tianjin, Nanchang, and other places. The company's products are of excellent quality and low prices. With the soaring gold prices and the resulting high prices of foreign goods, the company anticipates that sales this year will definitely be wider, so it has added more inventory to meet market demand.

The Ford Motor Company announces the grand opening ceremony of its new branch factory in Long Beach, California. This factory can be reached by waterway and railway, further integrating the company's various factories. This branch factory is designed to supply Southern California with Ford automobiles and trucks, and can produce 400 vehicles per day, which is far more than the now-closed Los Angeles branch factory, which could only produce 225 vehicles. The automobiles and trucks used by the company's new factory are transported from the Ford factories in Edgewater and Chester, using its own ships, through the Panama Canal, to Long Beach Port. There is a tunnel there that leads directly to the warehouse, where the vehicles are unloaded. From the time the ship docks to the time the car is manufactured, there is no wasted labor. The cranes, carriers, and machines used are far more effective than human labor. The Edgewater area is constructing a branch factory near the sea, and branch factories are also planned for Richmond and Seattle near the waterways.

Theater News 182

The Five Star Film Company announces that its first production was originally planned to start shooting earlier. The team members wanted to pursue true art to benefit society when it was released, so the script review was very strict. Now, the first one approved for shooting is "The Flying Hero of Lonely Mountain." "Exploring Linglong" will definitely be in the second production, and the second production will start filming around the 18th of this month.

The Wenge Bookstore at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Laobazi Road frankly states that the "Drunken Butterflies Among Flowers" photos are a new product newly shipped from the United States by the Lianyi Photo Company, exclusively managed and sold by this bookstore. Since the Nanjing Grand Theater screened this film, countless copies have been sold. There are very few in stock now, so purchasers should hurry. Those who admire the movie queen Janet Gaynor and the movie emperor Charles Farrell should not miss this opportunity. For mail orders, please include 10 cents per photo and send it to Mr. Yang Baidi, manager of Lianyi Photo Company, care of Tianya Painting Studio, 45 Baoshan Lane, Bin Tong Road, Zhabei.

The Star Film Company announces that after recently filming the entire fourteenth episode of "Burning the Red Lotus Temple," Zhang Youchuan will supervise a full team of talented actors, cameramen, scene designers, artists, etc., to continue filming the fifteenth episode of "Red Lotus Temple." The plot, the selected actors, and the clever shooting methods will all be new and different from the previous episodes. In the future, audiences who love "Red Lotus Temple" will have a fresh experience.

The National Grand Theater on Zhaopu Road and Haining Road announces that it will screen the unprecedentedly funny love film, "Two Heroes Compete for Beauty," starring the world-famous "Tall and Skinny" and "Little Dwarf" starting tomorrow. It will once again be a chaotic and crowded scene.

The Xifan Film Company announces that it is currently working hard to film a Qing Dynasty swordsman martial arts film, "Golden Rooster Ridge," which can be called the most successful great production of this year. The interior scenes have already been completed, and next week they will go to Ningbo to shoot exterior scenes. This film is very promising and can win glory for domestic films.

The Great China Film Company announces that the first night of the premiere of its historical epic "Stone Princess" and the added performance of the Amorous song and dance drama "Crab Shell Beauty" at the Central Grand Theater was sold out before 9 o'clock, so that later arrivals could not squeeze in. However, many people insisted on seeing it, causing the ticket collectors to have difficulty maintaining order and causing some chaos. Fortunately, the theater staff maintained order effectively, avoiding any problems. Now the company sees that this drama truly has the power to move stones, so today it has specially appointed company staff and actors Tang Yunqing, Gu Xiaowo, etc., to serve as temporary receptionists to better serve the audience.

Calligraphy and Painting News 184

The Beiping Lü Gongwang Writing and Fixed-Price General Receiving Office announces that Major General Lü Gongwang of Beiping's calligraphy has never been advertised for low prices since he was in Shanghai, but he is highly respected by all walks of life because it is rare to find a military man who is proficient in calligraphy. Recently, to assist with a certain charity event, a month-long fan-giving event was held. Taking advantage of this good opportunity, various ports inside and outside have requested screen couplets. Due to many requests, it was previously announced that the low prices would continue with an 80% discount on the gold standard. Therefore, the number of pieces in the past few days has been extremely large, and it is feared that the quota will soon be full again. Only those who are quick will get there first.

The Changming Art College announces that the number of students in each grade of the school in the previous semester was very small. However, since the principal Wang Yiting and all the professors were able to provide good guidance, the achievement exhibition held at the end of the semester was brilliant and well-received by public opinion. The number of students increased greatly during the summer class. The number of students actually attending this semester has also increased several times compared to the return semester. The school started classes yesterday. At 10 a.m., a supplementary commencement ceremony was held, and the ceremonies were performed as usual. Principal Wang first gave a speech, briefly stating that painting emphasizes skill and, more importantly, spirituality. Then, professors Wang, Wang, Song, and others gave speeches one after another. After the speeches, Principal Wang went to the podium again to discuss the relationship between Chinese and Western painting, as well as mutual reference and assistance. After the ceremony, Principal Wang went downstairs and painted a large-scale "Pine and Crane" painting on a whim, and provided painting methods at any time. Male and female students, looking up and surrounding the scene, were all happily delighted.

For the sake of popularization, the store continues to offer low prices, sacrificing its own capital to repay the kindness of patronage.
